               <div class="_8wo2"></div>
              </div>
              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Aquaponics
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The unique advantages of aquaponic systems are: 1. Conservation through constant water reuse and recycling. 2. Organic fertilization of plants with natural fish emulsion. (fish not exposed to heavy metals! Plants spared the dangerous chemicals in factory farming!) 3. The elimination of solid waste disposal from intensive aquaculture. 4. The reduction of needed cropland to produce like crops. 5. The overall reduction of environmental footprint for crop production. 6. Small efficient commercial installations can be built close to markets therefore reducing food miles. Some conceivable disadvantages with aquaponics are (and this group aims to address): 1. Initial expense for housing, tank, plumbing, pump/s, and grow beds. [Let's find cheaper ways!] 2. The infinite number of ways in which a system can be configured lends itself to equally varying results, conflicting research, and successes or failures. [Let's share info] 3. Some Aquaponic installations rely heavily on man-made energy, technology solutions, and environmental control to achieve recirculation and water/ambient temperatures [let's learn about systems designed with energy conservation in mind (such as utilizing solar heating and the exploitation of gravity to reduce pumping) to be energy efficient. 4. Whilst careful design can minimize the risk, Aquaponics systems can have multiple 'single points of failure' where problems such as an electrical failure or pipe blockage can lead to a complete loss of fish stock. [Let's explore how to minimize risk] 5. Often not closed loop [can we learn how to make growing duckweed and other methods easier/cheaper so we aren't tempted to buy fish food.
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">6.1&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">3 篇新帖</span></span>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 在美理財大家談
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 有鑒於來到美國的移民朋友, 希望能夠交換美國理財資訊, 本版於2014年 10月19日 設立. 為擴大資訊來源, 本版雖由台灣移民成立, 但歡迎所有年齡18歲以上之在美移民朋友, 不限制台灣移民參與. 為提供一個良好, 有效, 安全, 及合法意見交流環境, 凡加入本版的版員必須同意及遵守 以下po 文及發言規則. 不能同意並遵守以下發言者, 請即刻退出本討論區. 未離開本討論區的版員, 視為已同意以下po 文及發言規則. I. 廣告文禁止: 所有與在美國理財資訊無關的廣告文, 管理員將直接刪除並永久block 該貼文版友的版員資格. II. 與美國理財資訊無關po 文禁止: 所有與在美國理財資訊無關的po 文, 管理員將直接刪除. 管理員並會給予該貼文版友一次警告. 如再次張貼與在美國理財資訊無關的po 文, 管理員將直接刪除該版友版員資格. III. 公開集資貼文及討論禁止: 本版禁止任何在本版上公開集資的貼文或討論, 任何公開集資的貼文或討論, 管理員將直接刪除該貼文或討論並給予張貼版員警告一次. 如再次張貼公開集資的貼文或討論, 管理員將直接刪除該版友版員資格. IV. 人身攻擊禁止: 本版禁止任何對其他版員的人身攻擊言論. 凡違反版員, 管理員將僅給予警告一次. 當該版員再次違法本條規定時, 管理員將直接刪除其版員資格. V. 違反任何法規po 文及討論禁止: 所有任何可能違反各州州法或聯邦法的貼文, 管理員將直接刪除. 管理員並會給予該貼文版友一次警告. 如再次張貼任何可能違反各州州法或聯邦法的貼文或討論, 管理員將直接刪除該版友版員資格. VI. 轉貼他版禁止: 本版所有個人意見張貼, 非經張貼版友同意, 不得轉貼至其他網路討論區或個人臉書. 依經發現未經同意轉貼他版, 管理員將刪除該轉貼版友版員資格. VII. Block 管理員禁止: 凡管理員發現有任何版員block 管理員, 管理員將直接刪除該版友版員資格. 如再次加入, 再次被發現block管理員, 管理員將永久block 該版友加入本版資格. VIII. 管理員版規解釋權 : 當上述版規解釋有所爭議時, 管理員保有唯一的解釋權利, 且版員必須同意並遵守管理員的解釋. 此外, 請版友注意: (1) 本討論區僅提供一個理財資訊討論的平台, 本版管理員不為任何版友貼文及討論內容的真偽與否負擔任何責任(包含法律責任).請版友自行判定各貼文或討論內容的真實性跟可信度. (2) 本討論區為一個臉書理財資訊討論平台, 所有版員皆可閱讀並參與討論所有的貼文. 因此, 請勿在本討論區張貼或討論個人私密訊息. (3) 本討論區內所有貼文, 討論及建議皆僅供版員參考, 如有任何理財相關的專業問題 (例如報稅及設立公司等), 本版建議您仍要與各領域專業人士洽詢專業服務. (4) 本討論區內任何自稱專業人士的發言,皆為其個人意見, 不代表本版管理員意見, 本版也不為任何一為專業人士的發言背書. (5) 當本討論區內任何自稱專業人士的版友在版上回答任何版員提出的問題時 , 其所有發言皆不代表其已同意代表任何版員進行任何商業服務 (舉例: 當稅務律師回答某版友的問題時, 並不代表該稅務律師已同意代表該版友進行稅務相關業務). 如版友想要獲得某專業人士版友的服務, 請各版友自行pm 各專業人士版友洽詢. 感謝各版友閱讀, 同意並遵守以上各規則, 並祝福各位理財順利, 財源廣進!

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 The Real Cowboy 911
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Cowboy 911 is a worldwide group of people who pledge to offer assistance to others with livestock and pets in emergency situations. We offer a procedure manual and monetary assistance to facilitate the volunteers who rescue animals. Our members have specific skills, access, and equipment needed for livestock rescue. When disasters happen, thousands of small and large animals need evacuation and care. From pets to barnyard animals to wildlife. Assistance is needed when natural disasters strike. Ours is a voluntary movement, our members get involved in whatever capacity and skill they can offer. Volunteers are often the difference between life and death for the animals in need of evacuation. This is an immense service to the owners of these animals, many of whom feel their animals are family. In return the members of the group should be willing to do the same for each other, Because It's The Right Thing To Do! The Cowboy way. Helping another is its own reward. Let's get back to neighbors helping neighbors. After all, we are all friends and neighbors here!

                 〖主旨〗 大家好，這裡是一個讓大家了解美國選擇權的一個群組。這裡的目的 是希望讓你了解美國選擇權的實際交易方式，進而強化你的整體投資策略，讓大家在這裡可以共同成長學習。 同時也希望看到大家有互動式的問答，也就是除了我個人的分享，也期待看到大家的互動，不管是不同意見，還是提問題，讓大家可以確實從中獲益。 - 〖貼文分享規則〗 1.如果有人想來這邊為你的channel / 粉絲團打廣告可以視情況允許，前提是必須分享與美股/美股選擇權有關的看法 / 分析都可以，但如果只是直接打廣告我就直接刪除不通知了。 2.分享影片/文章時記得加註自己的見解，必須有一定長度，不能只是“不錯”兩個字帶過或甚至於空白，並且一樣要和美股/美股選擇權相關，不然也會被刪文喔。 謝謝！

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Make Money Online (MMO) - What Works And What doesn't Work With MMO
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to our Group - ONLY ENGLISH TEXT and we don't accept any kind of PORN, DATING AND NUDE CONTENT. Admin control. We don't allow any GOOGLE ADSENSE posts anymore since the massive porn and violent content on it. Everyone who will break the group rules will get a permanent ban and a report to facebook administration! Some simple rules to keep the group clean and popular: - NO PORN - NO DATING - NO GOOGLE ADSENSE - NO VIOLENT CONTENT - NO NUDE CONTENT - NO SCAM PROGRAMS - NO SPAM COMMENTS If we catch you breaking the rules, you will get a permanent ban from the group and in 75% we will send you a notice about it! Double accounts or massive accounts with the same names will all be reported and you will lose all of them! ------------------------------------------------------------- Making Money Online (MMO) can be a fantastic business and once you make that first sale – see that first sale/commission with your own eyes – you are going from a "Dreamer" to become a "BELIEVER". But a big problem is that more than 50% of those people who starts up with MMO don't have a “first sale” story. They can't tell their own story of how they now have faith in MMO......... Lack of skills, lack of a plan, and lack of motivation – are often three of the main reasons why people feel they are not succeeding with MMO. But the biggest problem of all with MMO is perhaps the INFORMATION OVERLOAD you receive all the time when doing MMO and searching for the best way to make your business. Very often with MMO you are pushed and pulled in every direction. There's always something new that is better than the new thing yesterday. There's always a loophole, or a marketing disaster, or some drastic must-know change with Google, or a new recently uncovered way to make money online...or....or...or... This is the reason why our purpose with this group is to create a network, where we can tip each other about what doesn't works and especially WHAT WORKS when you are working with Making Money Online (MMO). Therefore share your Tips and receive tips about MMO from other Group Members.

                 Social media marketing refers to the process of gaining website traffic or attention through social media sites. Social media marketing programs usually center on efforts to create content that attracts attention and encourages readers to share it with their social networks. A corporate message spreads from user to user and presumably resonates because it appears to come from a trusted, third-party source, as opposed to the brand or company itself. Hence, this form of marketing is driven by word-of-mouth, meaning it results in earned media rather than paid media. Social media has become a platform that is easily accessible to anyone with internet access. Increased communication for organizations fosters brand awareness and often, improved customer service. Additionally, social media serves as a relatively inexpensive platform for organizations to implement marketing campaigns. Through this group you can share your work/experiences in Social Media Marketing. You can also promote your content to gain website traffic. 
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Crowdfunding Marketing/Press/Buzz/Planning
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This Group is Dedicated to helping Crowdfunding Projects Creators with Marketing/Press/Buzz and Planning a Successful Campaign. Welcome! http://ayudos.com New ground rules for this Group! https://www.facebook.com/groups/crowdfundbuzz/ PLEASE FOLLOW or your LINK and Post will be deleted. 1. Only post links to crowdfunding projects on Kickstarter, Indiegogo or any other similar crowdfunding sites, and if you are crowdfunding on your own website. 2. No Donation or Charity projects. They will be deleted! (No exceptions) 3. Links to crowdfunding websites and blogs that have helpful tips and advice to help promote crowdfunding projects are ALLOWED to post. 4. DO NOT post links to Crowdfunding Promotion or marketing services!!! They are not allowed and they will be deleted! 5. Links to Crowdfunding industry related Events/ Webinars / Livestreams are allowed..for now. About Crowd funding https://www.facebook.com/pages/Crowd-funding/103741542997812 Crowdfunding (alternately crowd financing, equity crowdfunding, crowd-sourced fundraising) is the collective effort of individuals who network and pool their money, usually via the Internet, to support efforts initiated by other people or organizations. Crowdfunding is used in support of a wide variety of activities, including disaster relief, citizen journalism, support of artists by fans, political campaigns, startup company funding, motion picture promotion,free software development, inventions development, scientific research, and civic projects. Crowdfunding can also refer to the funding of a company by selling small amounts of equity to many investors. This form of crowdfunding has recently received attention from policymakers in the United States with direct mention in the JOBS Act; legislation that allows for a wider pool of small investors with fewer restrictions. While the JOBS Act awaits implementation, hybrid models, such as Mosaic Inc., are using existing securities laws to enable the public in approved states to invest directly in clean energy projects as part of a crowd. Crowdfunding has its origins in the concept of crowdsourcing, which is the broader concept of an individual reaching a goal by receiving and leveraging small contributions from many parties. Crowdfunding is the application of this concept to the collection of funds through small contributions from many parties in order to finance a particular project or venture. Crowdfunding models involve a variety of participants. They include the people or organizations that propose the ideas and/or projects to be funded, and the crowd of people who support the proposals. Crowdfunding is then supported by an organization (the "platform") which brings together the project initiator and the crowd.
                </div>
               </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Beekeeping for Beginners
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 YOU MUST ANSWER THE SCREENING QUESTIONS TO BE ACCEPTED! IF YOU DO NOT, YOUR REQUEST WILL BE DENIED. Beekeeping for Beginners is a group where you can learn more about beekeeping, ask questions from experienced beekeepers, and hopefully even learn something new if you've been beekeeping for years. I originally created this beekeeping group for my students and to market my online beekeeping and in-person beekeeping classes for my business Queen Bri's Honey Farm &amp; Bee Removal. As it grew in popularity with others on FaceBook who had not yet taken my classes, I decided to open it up to all new beginner beekeepers and any experienced beekeepers who wanted to join and help mentor others. In this group we discuss how to get started in beekeeping, books you should check out, classes we recommend, where you can buy beekeeping equipment, hive maintenance, pest control, how to feed your bees, how to harvest honey, new things or different ways of doing things that beekeepers are trying out in the beekeeping world, and how to get your bees best prepared to go into winter. Rules: 1) Please be respectful of others. Members who bully others will be removed from the group. 2) No non-related bee posts or for sale posts. 3) Instructors of beekeeping classes may make one post per week in the Discussion feed for their classes. 4) If you have something for sale that is not a class AND is bee-related, you may post this item or service in the comments section in our weekly Marketing Monday post. Any other sale post will be deleted, and if you do it again, you will be blocked from the group. 5) No promoting your own or others YouTube sites, FaceBook groups, or FaceBook pages. I did the work to build this group up without poaching off other people's groups that they worked hard to build. You can do the same. FaceBook has an advertising program - use it. These posts will be removed, and the person posting them will be removed and blocked from the group. 6) Discussion posts which frequently develop into negative discussions, such as Treatment Free or Flow Hive posts will be removed. These posts usually turn into name calling, nasty posts. My admins and I have day jobs. We don't have time to sit around all day to moderate discussions like this while they spiral out of control. They also frequently cause people to get pissed off and leave the group. Thus, these and other posts which the Admins deem to have the potential to blow up will be removed with no further explanation. Do not send an Admin a nasty FaceBook message if your post gets removed. This will result in your immediate removal from the group with no further explanation. Our #1 goal in this group is to keep it friendly to everyone. This rule helps accomplish that. I hope that you will learn a lot from this group, and thanks for your interest in joining! Founder and Admin Tonya Leathers Wells www.queenbrishoney.com

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Actors, Filmmakers, &amp; Job Postings!
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 WHAT CAN BE POSTED TO THE WALL: Jobs and ONLY Jobs on the Wall! Acceptable Job Postings are: Film (feature, short, etc...) TV / Web Series or Pilots, Commercials, and Plays. Note: this Facebook group is primarily intended for the American, European, and Australian film making community, jobs outside these regions need to have enough compensation to at least cover travel and housing for these filmmakers. Once submitted allow about 24 hours for the job to be approved and posted, although this is usually much faster. Unacceptable postings are anything else! (This includes reality TV jobs and acting workshops.) Posting spam jobs will have you blocked and banned without a second chance. WHEN POSTING A JOB FOLLOW THIS FORMAT: TITLE &amp; TYPE: Feature, Pilot, Play, Short, Commercial, etc... CASTING: Gender, Age-Range, etc... and/or CREW CALL: Cinematographer, Sound Mixer, etc... LOCATION: City, State, Country (Do not say Starbucks on 7th!) COMPENSATION (clearly state: paying, non-paying, etc...) CONTACT (must include your email)! TIME(s): submission deadline, audition &amp; production time-frames Then below: ANYTHING ELSE! union status, requirements, links, etc... * Note: If the dates are firm and the job is paying $50/day or more, you are qualified to make your Job Posting an Event, therefore it will show up on the Wall like all the other Job Postings, but it will also show up on the event calendar.) ** Further note: There are 6 required lines. Put each item on it's own line and do not double space the lines! HOW TO PROMOTE YOURSELF: Upload your HEADSHOTS to PHOTOS put them in an ALBUM with your name and occupation as the Title and your info, contacts, and links as the Description. Upload your DEMO REELS to PHOTOS also. And upload your RESUMES to FILES! Make sure your File Name includes your name and your field of work i.e.: John-Doe_Actor.pdf NO CROWDFUNDING OR FINANCING: Posting about crowd funding, even posting for executive producers or producers to find you money is prohibited. Posting for money may cause you to be you blocked and banned without a second chance. NO BEGGING FOR LIKES GENERAL RULES: All posts must be in English albeit you may include a translation (in the same post below the English text). WARNING: Even though this group is moderated, it does not mean that anything on this group is accurate. Moderation is mostly an attempt to keep posters to follow the posting standards. The users of this group are responsible for all its content and all their interactions. The group is not and will not be liable for anything said or done by its users. FINAL NOTE: If you figure out a way to get your own unacceptable jobs or self promotions on the wall… (No I'm not going to tell you how to do it…) But if you figure it out and do it, you will be blocked and banned without a second chance. 
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Membership &amp; Subscription Site Community by Stu McLaren
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 This is a community-supported group hosted by Stu McLaren, founder of the TRIBE Experience for membership &amp; subscription site owners and future owners. Here are some guidelines that are important to follow in order to make this a supportive and productive group for everyone. 1. Administrators have the right and will utilize the option to delete comments or block all involvement in this group for any reason. 2. No direct or indirect self-promotion of your programs, groups or services, including no links to your site(s) or social media profiles and no PMing to solicit members or suggesting someone PMs you unless specifically requested by an admin. 3. No affiliate links. You may share a tool, program or service, that you love and use, but please no affiliate links in the group or DMs. 4. No lives, stories, GIFs, or uploaded videos in the group. GIFs can be used in comments but not in the original post. 5. Stay relevant. Posts not related to membership and subscription sites are not allowed. 6. No market research. You may not use this group to conduct market research for your own products and services. 7. Let's have some fun! Post your wins, questions, and challenges. Support others, seek support and most of all make progress on your membership sites. P.S. Any posts that violate the above rules will be deleted without notice. In summary... just be cool. 😎

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Market Gardening Success Group
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Welcome to the Market Gardening Success Group! This is a space for small acreage market gardeners to share innovations &amp; stories. It's also a place where you can ask an experienced group of farmers for advice and ideas. New farmers are welcome here! The goal of this group is to encourage, inspire and share our best practices with each other. We have high hopes that this model of farming is going to replace the old one, and that mass production of food will be replaced by production by the masses. Let's support each other along the way! A couple guidelines: 1. Please search the group (and the internet) first before asking a question, especially if the question steers toward the novice side of things. 2. If you wish to follow a post, use the menu (look for the three dots) at the top of the post to turn on notifications – comments of the form “following” or “.” clutter things up. 3. Keep your posts and comments on the topic of market gardening. Don’t be argumentative about methods and philosophies you disagree with, rather share your experience and why it works for you. This is not a place to push your agenda. 4. Sharing links and posts is OK, but they should be directly related to market gardening and not political in nature. Try to avoid “sharing” posts from your own page repeatedly, rather post directly on the group page if you have something to share with the group. 5. You can let the group know if you have market gardening items for sale, but don’t post the same thing repeatedly.
                </div>

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 PLEASE READ FULLY BEFORE POSTING TO THE GROUP ABOUT: Regenerative Agriculture Facebook Group exists to encourage “practical” discussion of all sustainable and regenerative agriculture “techniques and methods”. This includes permaculture, restoration agriculture, urban farming, spin farming and basically any and all methods of agricultural production that encourages regenerative treatment of the land. This means anybody starting out on the journey towards sustainable and regenerative practices are encouraged to be involved. To some, these people may not be “there yet” or “not good enough to qualify”. If you have a problem with someone learning a new skill such as brewing or gardening and using less than optimal methods, you may consider looking elsewhere or just ignoring those posts. We are all on a sliding scale of accomplishment and abilities. We are about the progression towards betterment, not the unobtainable goal of perfection. Expect seasonality with member interests. If you are tired of seeing the same kinds of things, scroll past them, please don't complain. THE FOLLOWING TOPICS ARE STRICTLY PROHIBITED: - Social Justice - GMO's - Glyphosate/Roundup - Politics - Global Warming/Climate Change or any derivation of that topic or subject RULES: 1. DO NOT complain about others or belittle someone for doing something in a way that is different than the way you do it. If you don't have something nice to say, don't say anything at all. We invite the wanna-be, the beginner and the experienced. 2. If a moderator or admin informs you that your post is in violation and is gracious enough to allow you to modify it to fit group parameters you have two options, modify as instructed, or delete the post. If you argue or inform the admin/moderator that you don't agree, you will be banned immediately. This is not a democracy and you don't get a vote. 3. No creating threads (opinion or otherwise) about a deleted post. If a post has been deleted, don't create a new thread to talk about it. If you want to ask why, please pm a moderator. The reason is you most likely posted one of the prohibited topics. 4. No meat eater bashing &amp; no vegan/vegetarian bashing. Both are welcome but neither side being hateful or disparaging of the other is tolerated. 5. DO NOT complain about the Admins/Mods. Enforcement of the rules will be at the discretion of the Admins and Moderators online at the time. We'll make mistakes &amp; you will hate us, we get that but please keep it to yourself. 6. If it does not directly pertain to the stated purpose of the group assume it will be deleted. 7. If you block any of the Admins or Moderators you will be banned permanently and immediately. ADMIN CONTACT – The Admins and Moderators will NOT debate, defend or argue with a member on the wall. If you are wondering why a post was removed, send a private message. Any disrespect shown an Admin or moderator can result in immediate removal. Thank You, Management

Do not put up postings for clothes, living room sets, lawn mowers, etc. If you are a company selling/building structures, please limit your main postings to once every seven days. You may add as many "replys" as you want to these postings during that time period. This is to prevent this group from being overrun by "advertisements" in a 'spammy' sort of way. Happy house hunting!!

                 This group is intended for freelance film professionals. Here we can ask questions of each other, network, look for jobs and hire crew. IN ADDITION, self promotion posts are not permitted, as they add a ton of clutter, and thereby the actual JOB POSTS get buried and people don't see them, and real opportunities are missed. We ask that you respect each other and pay for the services you require at group minimum or higher rates. We, like many of you grew tired of copy, credit, meal, posts on craigslist, other sites, and other Facebook groups. So, we therefore require than no gig be posted for less than $275 for a 12 hour day. If the day irs shorter, the group still mandates a $275/day minimum. If the day is longer, the rate should go up accordingly. In addition to our rate minimums, it must be clarified that these minimums DO NOT include and CANNOT include gear rental, kit fees, or materials fees. Such fees must be in addition to the labor rate. So, be sure to bear that in mind when posting. You have two options. One, you can post a set fee for gear, in addition to whatever labor rate you post. Two, you can post that you understand such fees are an extra cost and said fees can be negotiated privately. Finally, we may one exception to the rate minimum rules. We set a separate minimum, $210/12 hour day, for PAs. If more than 12 hours, you have to offer more. FINALLY. Because there is so much commotion whenever rates are not listed in a post, the following is the new policy. You cannot simply state "negotiable." Instead, you must acknowledge in writing, in your post, that the rate is negotiable, but will be no less than $275/12 hours. ALSO, it is illegal to post seeking a specific ethnicity, age, gender or someone of preferred sexual orientation. Any favoritism shown in this regard, no matter how minor, will get your post removed. Depending upon the situation, it may get you removed from the group. PLEASE no diatribe posts. In the case of violation, REPORT the post to ADMIN, and even tag myself, or another admin, like Cricket or KB. If we catch a post that does not conform to the labor rate minimum policies and fee policies, it will removed. If your post violates labor/discrimination law, it will be removed, and you may be removed along with it. People asking to join the page with obviously fake names/accounts will be rejected. There are three questions to answer. Finally, if you violate rules, there may be a PM sent assuming we believe the violation is an accident, but remember, we are busy, and it a courtesy, not a requirement. If it is felt the violation was made in spite of rules, you will be immediately removed permanently from the group.

SOME THINGS TO REMEMBER: If we delete your "Thank you for adding me " Post...That is our way of saying "You are very welcome" We saw it and recognized it but have to keep the wall clear If we delete your QUESTION it may be because there are multiple of the same Question and we picked one to answer and comment on...So, No offense...We're just trying to keep things nice and neat and maintain the flow of information Try to avoid unnecessary comments on old posts...Adding useful info is GREAT but sometimes there is no need to bump an older post back up top.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Search Marketing Mastermind is a group of some of the world’s best actively sharing their thoughts, ideas, and problems openly. This is a SAFE environment for SEO’s to ask questions, discuss best practices, and trends that help all users grow. Our goal is to help educate people about SEO, continuously improve, and speak with one voice in a wide-open industry. We are a fact-based group and try to maintain close relationships with search engines while citing patents to be as close as possible to facts when publishing content. Please feel free to ask questions if you feel the information you found on search is vague and you still are unsure after looking at articles. We fully understand that popular search engines like Google and Bing change upwards of 500 times a year tweaking their signals. We all post questions and have a problem with SEO as it’s forever changing. The power of 16,000 people is the probability that one of us at one time or another has experienced a similar problem. Feel free to post articles that contribute if it’s: • UNIQUE • Actionable • Above Basic Level (Overdone) • Links to credible resources (facts) • Gives credit to the source • Uses relevant &amp; timely research data • Solves a problem • Comes from an authoritative resource • Doesn’t make claims without evidence. *** Overly self-promotional content (sales material requires admin permission and is generally rejected) *** No sales or self-promotional material in here, please. This may result in immediate removal from the group. Content referenced or discussed should be beneficial to members. If someone is specifically asking about tools, what others are using for specific tasks etc this is an opportunity to post. If you feel unsure about whether it’s safe then ask one of our 25 group admins and we’ll be happy to answer. We don’t allow trolls in the group at all. If you disagree with a point made in the group then defend your thoughts eloquently with facts, references, and citations to information that will help us all to overcome myths commonly seen in the industry. Please ensure you’re being respectful of the group members and their knowledge as they’re not being compensated for being here. If you’re new to SEO: https://support.google.com/webmasters/answer/7451184?hl=en https://moz.com/beginners-guide-to-seo https://www.equinetacademy.com/seo-tutorial-step-step-search-engine-optimization-guide/ Spam and asking for likes to pages etc will result in permanent bans.

               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Small Farm, Sustainability &amp; Homestead Living
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Read Before You Post!! GROUP RULES &amp; DESCRIPTION This group is intended to be a place for the exchange of information, skills and ideas that can effect the small land holder, homesteader &amp; traditional farm family. It is, however, open to all. We invite the wanna-be, the beginner and the experienced. We hope to inspire those without a homestead to start living as if they do. We will focus on topics of sustainability, gardening, organic practices, and homemade &amp; homegrown foods... as well as making do, by making it at home. It is a reality based group. If you can't handle death and all of it's horribleness then a farm may not be for you. If you need a cutesy No Blood Page, there are plenty of vegan sustainable living pages. We have so many posts on spiders, snakes, insects, etc..., we ask that you do some real area research. Please do not ask, "What is this?", "What's it worth?", "What state is best for..." Do more with less... Do more for yourself. THE RULES- If it does not directly pertain to homesteading assume it will be deleted. If you have something to buy, sell or trade (or give away), please do not post it here. This page is not a classifieds community. DO NOT SELL YOUR STUFF ON HERE! If it looks like, smells like or we hear whispers of promotion, you're gone. And... do not use this group as a platform to promote your website, FB page, group or cause. Even if you link to something free (Amazon, eBay, etc...), if it has a referral-code, it will be deleted. Simply put... remove the referral-code. DO NOT complain about others or belittle someone for doing something in a way that is different than the way you do it. And no creating threads (opinion or otherwise) about other posts. If a post has been deleted, don't ask why. No politics... No religion... No rhetoric... and No drama. If you like that stuff, post it on your personal page - your friends love that. If you are not making posts that will help the group and its members, you are posting to harm the group and its members. Please keep posts relevant to the group's title/name. Shout-outs, pet pics, viral cartoons, videos or memes are not considered relevant to the group. Naming your farm or animal is not considered relevant. Don't post/comment for the sake of posting. Make it mean something to others. Photos posted should belong to you, please explain them (not just label). #ThisAin'tTwitter DO NOT feature children in photos. If you want to connect/discuss things with others in your area, visit your region's Chapter Group (https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=10202431850181784&amp;set=gm.10152839343713065&amp;type=1) No ALL CAPS! DO NOT complain about the Admins/Mods.. They're doing the best they can. Enforcement of the rules will be at the discretion of the Admins online at the time. We'll make mistakes &amp; you will hate us, we get that. To contact an admin: Go to 'Members' area, then CLICK on 'Admins' TY for being part of this great group. ~ADMIN

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 The Black Business Network Group (BBNG) is created to provide a platform for black business owners, creators, entrepreneurs and sellers to network together and build their businesses. We aim to provide an environment that will encourage creativity within the black community and provide a veritable marketplace for us to grow our businesses by encouraging the black community to make us their first point of contact for any and all their business and professional needs. We also aim to provide a platform that will adequately educate our community on financial matters and on how to create generational wealth, and will also inform us of all the better wealth-making/investment opportunities that are available to us. Ultimately, we intend to help build our black communities by making productive outreach into and investments in our communities nationwide. #OurNetWorthIsTheProductOfOurNetwork #YourNetWorthOurNetwork #OurPeopleOurCommunity #NoOneCanBuildUsUpButUs #WeHaveToComeTogetherToBuildUsTogether #WeAreAllWeveGot #WeAreNOBODYWithoutEconomicEmpowerment #ItsNotEnoughToJustBeBlackNProudWeShouldAlsoBeBlackNProminent

                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 I created this group because i own 5 acres but dont live on it yet so i wanted to see how other people live their lives on their land. We have people in here that might only work on a quarter acre and do a lot with it and some have all the way up to 250 Acres!! Everyone lives such different lives and there is no right or wrong way just whatever works best for you and your family!! If you do Homegrown. Store bought. Farm fresh. At home butchering. Animals to eat. Animals for pets. Plant based diets. Meat eaters. Believers or non believers. This group is about just living life and having a positive support group!! Building each other up! Offering love and support in a kind helpful way. There are no guidlines to the way everyone lives their lives!! Each one of us is different. We do what is best for ourselves and our family. I love seeing all the posts about food ,animals, snow, barns, trees, gardens, houses, tractors, ponds, camp fires, i could go on forever! I love hearing about the daily life of good people. I love seeing people happy n living life the way they choose!! Be kind to one another!! 🌳🌳🌳🌳🌳🏡🌳🌳🌳🌳🌳 "A friendly place for all to share knowledge about 5 acre living. 5 acres aren't required but an open mind and kind heart are. " Rules: Be kind, no rudeness or name calling tolerated. Just tag an admin or hit report. No animal sales or any sales. We have a group for sales called 5 Acre Business. Any bloody or gory post put a Warning on top and add pictures in comments. No spammy posts and links. Please no Gofundme links, soliciting members or fundraising type posts Leave politics and religion at door No sharing of personal groups or pages on group wall unless approved by admin. View our pinned post to share your personal groups or pages. We have a group for all real estate listings called 5 Acre Realty Group Know that most people have the best intentions and treat them as such (including admins) If you ask and question and get your answer please turn off comments (you won't receive anymore notifications and comments but the info stays searchable for others) I do not like controversy. You may post in Spanish, but an English translation must be included to be approved. Posts by businesses who are posting for the sake of advertising their own business will be deleted. They clog the feed and people cannot find the actual Job postings. Besides, most people here are not working, therefore they are not shopping. Plain and simple. Please do not post your Work Wanted ads here. The majority of people here are also looking for work. If every single person here puts an ad for what type of work they are looking for, no one will be able to find the ACTUAL job ads. From now on, those posts will be deleted. Thanks everyone! Est.                  Affiliate Marketing Review
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 NOTE: Group is open for members pinned post. Get more exposure to your offer for the price of a cup of coffee and you will also receive a home based business report and marketing tool to grow and build your business. If you are a serious business minded you would appreciate the benefit of getting exposure...Advertisement. NO SPAMMING ALLOWED, IF YOU ARE AUTO POSTING YOU CAN NOT BE GETTING ANY RESULTS. BE HUMAN, BE YOURSELF. DO NOT ATTACH A LINK TO OTHER PEOPLES POST. IF YOU DO YOUR POST WILL BE REMOVED. REPEAT YOU WILL BE BLOCKED FROM THE GROUP. http://www.socialknacks.com NO NUDITY! All Post are screened! Learn How To Become A Great Affiliate Marketer Create a strong website based on something you enjoy, and then make money using affiliate ads. This article will provide some great tips to help you grow your affiliate website. http://www.socialknacks.com Try to see how affiliated companies track outside orders. If you send sales orders to a company that ultimately take place over the phone or through the mail, and your affiliate ID is not on them, you will not get your commission, which could really add up over time. If you generated significant profits, consider requesting more money from your program. If you are able to generate sales and are able to market successfully, the program will want to keep you on board and will do whatever it takes. To maximize the profitability of your affiliate network, drop affiliates that are not performing up to standard. Keep an eye on your affiliates to make sure that they are performing well. Cutting ties with underperforming affiliates gives you room to add more ambitious partners. If you pick an affiliate that has a lot of options on how to get your money, it is the best way. Some companies will pay through PayPal and AlertPay, while others mail checks. http://www.socialknacks.com Secret links are links that allow you utilize affiliate links without being blatantly obvious. Certain techniques can help you weave affiliate links throughout your text without making the links obvious. Make use of these techniques, but always be honest and upfront about it. Be sure that potential customers do not feel duped by content that is irrelevant... Get Marketing Advice and build your business go to this link for more: http://www.socialknacks.com

              <div class="_8tn0">
               <div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Affiliate Marketing
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Affiliate marketing is a type of performance-based marketing in which a business rewards one or more affiliates for each visitor or customer brought about by the affiliate's own marketing efforts. The industry has four core players: the merchant (also known as 'retailer' or 'brand'), the network (that contains offers for the affiliate to choose from and also takes care of the payments), the publisher (also known as 'the affiliate'), and the customer. The market has grown in complexity to warrant a secondary tier of players, including affiliate management agencies, super-affiliates and specialized third party vendors.
                </div>
               </div>
               <div>
                <div class="_8um4">
                 <span class="_8ul_"><i class="_8wo5 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_8f3bf5"></i><span class="_8um1">6.3&nbsp;万位成员</span></span><span class="_8um0"><i class="_8wo6 _8wos img sp_oDRLRzjLfgY sx_ce40e2"></i><span class="_8um2">72 篇新帖</span></span>

                 Welcome to the Boss Project! How to get the most out of this community: 1. SHARE: Share your successes, tips, tricks and favorite resources. We know you’re a wildly talented group. We want to help you celebrate and create opportunities for you to share your expertise. Remember to add VALUE not links. P.S. Direct promo links are not allowed (ever). Please, focus on showing up and SERVING when you can help. Only Admins or approved guests can go LIVE, any LIVE videos that haven't gotten approval will be deleted. 2. ASK: Don’t hide behind your keyboard. Ask questions! Try to be very specific in your question to help us help you. When asking for feedback on your website, blog, social media, products or services DO NOT link them. Post a screenshot of what you’re referencing instead. Linked posts will be deleted. ABOUT BOSS PROJECT + YOUR HOSTS This community is hosted by us, Abagail Pumphrey and Emylee Williams. We are here to support, motivate and encourage you all. We will be sharing updates, fun announcements and occasionally sharing our services. By being a part of this group you will always be the first to know! COMMUNITY GUIDELINES BE KIND: Negative attitudes can be checked at the door. Rude comments or foul language will not be tolerated. That doesn’t mean you can’t share when you have a bad day, let’s just try to be upbeat. If your post is solely about “venting” without a silver lining or a lesson learned that might help someone else it may get deleted. BE CARING: Support others and they will support you back. The more you give, the more you will get out of the group. Even if you can’t answer someone’s question specifically give some encouraging words on their post. PROMO RULES: Please do not continuously promote yourself. If you try to get sneaky with your promotion by disguising it as a regular post OR "market research" it WILL get deleted. Do not post your direct link (ever). Do not write long form "blog" type posts disguised as helpful. Do not ask people to PM you. Just don't. This is NOT the place to repost the content you are publishing on your social media accounts. These posts WILL get deleted and if you keep at it, you will get removed from the group. ABSOLUTELY NO LINK SHARING THREADS. This means any form of “comment with your email address to hear about ____” or “leave your social media handle below so I can follow you” or “email me if you want to guest post on my blog or collaborate”. We provide threads for these very things for you so there’s no need to create your own (it just bogs everything down). P.S. Direct promo links are not allowed (ever). At the end of the day be a nice person and always come from the place of GIVING, not GETTING. We reserve the right to delete and remove and post and/or person without notice.

                 Livestock Born Different
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 Livestock Born Different On the lookout for livestock born different! I am currently in the research phase of a book, and looking to acquire specimens that I can photograph and feature in it. Seeking all types of livestock including cattle, horses, llamas, alpacas, goats, sheep, pigs, rabbits and poultry. Looking for all types of deformities, from the simple to the weird. We always purchase specimens. We also offer custom preservations if you would like to keep your specimen but still have it featured in the book. This include traditional taxidermy, wet preservation and freeze drying. Please check out the files for more information on preserving your specimen for sale or preservation. Feel free to post photos of any critter you have a question about, I will do my best to answer any questions. Thank you! Your support in this project is greatly appreciated. Shelby The Rules: As a small business owner and livestock owner, I do not always get a lot of spare internet time. As a result it may take as much as 24 hours for me to address an issue. Please be patient. 1. Don't belittle, insult, berate, put down, or bash any other member for their decisions or choices. Nasty, offensive or hate related comments are not constructive and will be deleted. This is an educational group and let us all do our part to keep it that way. 2. If you see any possible violations of Rule 1, Please either Tag me or use the option to report to Admin. Do not report to facebook, this will not get the issue resolved. 3. Posts of NON Livestock subjects ( Dogs, Cats, Horses, Reptiles etc) will be locked on a daily basis so no comments can be made, Posts will remain in a view only format. This group is strictly for discussing Livestock and will be limited to the following species: Cattle, Sheep, Goats, Pigs, Rabbits, Poultry, Llamas, Alpacas. 4. Off topic posts- Including livestock for sale, posts asking for identification of a random item, etc. Will be deleted. If you post the same thing repeatedly you will be removed from the group. Currently we only have 38 permanently banned members and I would like to keep it that way. 5. Constructive criticism is allowed if done in a polite manner. Please consider your posts before posting impulsively. If you don't agree with someone share some evidence as to why you believe differently and leave it at that. No one likes the "Because I Said so!" defense. Give a reason. Present the facts. 6. Posts may not be shared outside the group without permission of the OP. Not by direct share or by Screen capture. Questions or comments? Feel free to PM me or post them below. I will do my best to answer them.

                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 We welcome all women in ag who are here to talk about all things ag with a positive attitude and can follow the rules. Please come share your knowledge or learn a little more. If you see a post that violates our rules, click on the down arrow to the right of the questionable post and select, "Report to admin." This will result in the fastest response from an admin. You may PM an admin, response time may vary from minutes to days. 01 - Sales This is not a buy/sell/trade group. Posts or comments with links selling anything will be deleted. 02 - Agriculture topics All posts must be related to ag, keep discussions positive, on topic, &amp; focused on ag. No anti-ag posts or comments. Personal attacks, profanity, mean, or rude comments may result in removal from WIA 03 - Treatment of animals No displaying or suggesting cruelty, harmful, dangerous, or illegal activity. Illegal in many or all states; cockfighting, killing birds of prey, killing venomous snakes, relocating nuisance animals 04 - Private Messages No member shall send another member unsolicited PM (private message) of any kind. 05- Controversial topics No rants or controversial topics that create drama; politics, GMO, religion, animal rights, killing, or other propaganda. No posts or comments complaining about a post, person, business, group, admin, 06 - Photo subjects Photos of dead animals, bodily injuries or injured animals can be posted in comments if needed but please minimize the posting of gruesome photos to avoid giving activists propaganda. 07 - Solicitation No solicitation for funds (GoFundMe, etc.), solicitation of free stuff, petitions, contests, requests for votes, requests to name something, surveys 08 - Promotion No self promotion, fund-raisers, job listings, blogs, farms, businesses listings, social media, dating ads, excessive posting, links to facebook groups, etc 09 - Photo ownership &amp; logos Please ask permission prior to sharing photos or information from this page. Posts with photos must be your property. Watermarks or logos bigger than 5% of the image are not permitted. 10 - Blocking No blocking an admin or moderator. These rules have evolved out of necessity. The admins/mods are volunteers. We may close posts early if we are unable to motor hot topics. There will be potentially grisly pictures on posts at times (fecal matter, underdeveloped embryos, etc.) although is this a natural aspect of agriculture, for some it is disturbing. We ask that you turn off notifications for this page if you find them cringe-worthy, thus eliminating them from your regular newsfeed. For the privacy of our members, joint accounts or business/farm accounts are not permitted. Failure to follow the rules will result removal from the group, without warning.

                <div class="mvm uiP _8s__ fsm">
                 Nannies And Housekeepers In LA
                </div>
                <div class="mvm uiP _8t00 fsm">
                 To Join / Stay: 1. You MUST answer entry questions and agree to the rules, if you don’t you’ll be declined . 2. Post what you are looking for within 24 hours 3. Please delete / answer on your post to people who comment to let them know if you are no longer searching or if you still are. 4. No repeat posts. You can type bump on your original post to move it back to the top of the discussion board. 5. We must be able to see your profile picture. Disclaimer: Nannies And Housekeepers in LA is an information source only. We do not place nannies (NOT an agency) nor do we do employment contracts or problem solving. Any information posted is by individual persons and is not validated or verified so trust the information viewed at your own risk. Agencies are limited to finding nannies NOT advertise their service to parents, unless requested by parents first. Rules of the page: - FILES: THESE ARE FOR NANNIES/ HOUSEKEEPERS TO SHARE JOBS WITH EACH OTHER ON BEHALF OF PEOPLE MAYBE NOT IN THIS GROUP. - If you are a Nannies/housekeepers searching for a new family please post the information you feel comfortable. We recommend your name, areas you are willing to serve, full or part time, and years of experience. This is essentially a public page so do not provide detailed personal information. It is your responsibility to remove your post once you have accepted a position. - if you are a parent searching for a Nannies/housekeepers you can look at the available nannies or list your job. We recommend your general location (not specific address), full or part time, and number of children. -if you plan to upload a document under files, please run if by one of the Admins for approval, otherwise it will be deleted. -If information is shared that we deem to be either too personal or inappropriate for this page we reserve the right to delete the post, this includes anything off topic from what this group is intended for including advertisement for an agency or personal business. ABSOLUTELY NO aggressive agency marketing. UNLESS a parent ASKS about an agency, limited commenting under their posts is required. This place is for non agency folks to refer each other. If you would like to recruit staff that is okay. **DO NOT REFER PEOPLE WHO ARE NOT IN THIS GROUP. ALL INQUIRIES MUST BE FROM GROUP MEMBERS ONLY, IF YOU CAN'T TAG THEM DIRECTLY, PLEASE DON'T PUT THEIR INFORMATION ON COMMENTS OR POSTS** ***Inability to comply within the group guidelines will results in removal from the group without warning, and guidelines are subject to change for the betterment of the group***
